CLAUDE.md","","This file provides guidance to Claude Code (claude.ai/code) when working with code in this repository.","","## Project Overview","","openGauss is an open-source relational database management system with high performance, full-chain security, and intelligent operations. It's developed by Huawei with optimizations for ARM architecture and multi-core systems.","","## Architecture","","### Core Components","- **src/gausskernel/**: Core database kernel","- **src/common/**: Common utilities and libraries","- **src/bin/**: Binary executables (psql, gs_initdb, etc.)","- **contrib/**: Extension modules and additional components","- **src/include/**: Header files for the entire project","","### Key Directories","- **build/**: Build system scripts and configuration","- **src/test/**: Comprehensive test suites including regression, isolation, and performance tests","- **doc/**: Documentation and architectural diagrams","- **simpleInstall/**: Simple installation scripts for quick setup","","## Build Commands","","### Prerequisites","Download and extract binarylibs (third-party dependencies) to the project directory or specify path with `-3rd`.","","### Primary Build Command","```bash","./build.sh -m [debug|release|memcheck] -3rd [binarylibs_path]","```","","**Build modes:**","- `release`: Optimized production build (default)","- `debug`: Debug build with additional debugging info","- `memcheck`: Debug build with ASAN memory checking","","### Build Options","- `--cmake`: Use cmake instead of traditional configure/make","- `-pkg`/`--package`: Create installation package after build","- `-nopt`: Disable ARM LSE optimizations (for older ARM platforms)","- `-T`/`--tassl`: Build with TaSSL support","- `-nls`/`--enable_nls`: Enable Native Language Support","","### Examples","```bash","# Basic release build","./build.sh","","# Debug build with specific binarylibs path","./build.sh -m debug -3rd /path/to/binarylibs","","# Create installation package","./build.sh -pkg","","# Use cmake build system","./build.sh --cmake","```","","### Build Output","- Compiled binaries: `dest/bin/`","- Installation path: `dest/`","- Build logs: `make_compile.log`","","## Testing","","### Regression Tests","```bash","cd src/test/regress","make check","```","","### Specific Test Suites","- **Isolation tests**: `src/test/isolation/`","- **HA tests**: `src/test/ha/`","- **Performance tests**: `src/test/performance/`","","### Test Schedules","Different parallel test schedules available:","- `parallel_schedule`: Main regression test suite","- `parallel_schedule0`: Core functionality tests","- Various specialized schedules for specific features","","## Development Workflow","","### Configuration","The project uses autoconf/configure for traditional builds:","```bash","./configure --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS [options]","make -sj","make install -sj","```","","### CMake Alternative","For faster builds:","```bash","mkdir cmake_build \u0026\u0026 cd cmake_build","cmake .. -DENABLE_MULTIPLE_NODES=OFF -DENABLE_THREAD_SAFETY=ON","make -sj \u0026\u0026 make install -sj","```","","### Code Organization","- C/C++ source primarily in `src/gausskernel/`","- SQL extension scripts in `contrib/*/sql/`","- Test data and expected outputs in respective `data/` and `expected/` directories","","## Database Features","","### Storage Engines","- **Standard row storage**: Traditional PostgreSQL-compatible storage","- **Column store**: Optimized for analytical workloads","- **MOT (Memory Optimized Tables)**: In-memory storage engine","","### Performance Optimizations","- Multi-core NUMA-aware architecture","- ARM instruction optimizations","- SQL bypass for simplified execution","- Parallel recovery mechanisms","","### Security Features","- Full encryption support","- Account management and authentication","- Operation auditing capabilities","- Privilege management","","## Installation","","The project supports multiple installation methods:","- **Enterprise installation**: Using gs_preinstall and gs_install scripts","- **Simple installation**: Using scripts in `simpleInstall/`","- **Docker installation**: Using dockerfiles in `docker/`","","Note: Installation requires proper environment setup including user creation, directory permissions, and network configuration as detailed in the README.","","## Parallel Materialization Optimization","","### Overview","Recently implemented parallel Materialize node optimization provides \"serialize once, serve many\" capability for high-performance analytical workloads. This addresses the performance bottleneck where multiple similar queries execute redundant materialization work.","","### Key Features","","#### Lock-free Circular Buffer","- **Location**: `src/gausskernel/runtime/executor/parallelMaterial.cpp`","- **Implementation**: Multi-producer/multi-consumer atomic operations","- **Benefits**: Eliminates contention in `seq_scan_getnext`/`heap_getnext` calls","- **Configuration**: Automatically enabled for 2+ parallel workers","","#### Partition-wise Parallelism","- **Integration**: Uses existing `ispwj` flag infrastructure","- **Worker Distribution**: Dynamic load balancing with work stealing","- **Memory Isolation**: Per-partition tuple stores with independent memory management","- **Scalability**: Reduces data volume per worker through partition assignment","","#### Per-worker Memory Management","- **Allocation**: `CalculateWorkerMemory()` distributes 80% of total memory across workers","- **Minimum**: 1MB per worker guaranteed","- **Spill Handling**: Automatic context reset when worker memory exceeded","- **Tuning**: Integrates with existing `work_mem` (openGauss `sort_mem`) parameters","","### Configuration Parameters","","#### Enable Parallel Materialization","```sql","-- Enable parallel query execution","SET enable_parallel_query = on;","","-- Set maximum workers per gather operation  ","SET max_parallel_workers_per_gather = 8;","","-- Adjust memory allocation per operation","SET work_mem = '256MB';","```","","#### Performance Tuning","```sql","-- For partition-wise operations","SET enable_partition_wise_join = on;","SET enable_partition_wise_agg = on;","","-- Memory pressure thresholds","SET parallel_tuple_fraction = 0.1;","SET sort_mem = '512MB';  -- openGauss equivalent of work_mem","```","","### Architecture Integration","","#### Executor Node Path","- **Entry Point**: `ExecMaterial()` in `nodeMaterial.cpp:277`","- **Parallel Dispatch**: `ExecParallelMaterial()` coordinates worker roles","- **Producer Logic**: `ExecParallelMaterialProducer()` handles tuple generation","- **Consumer Logic**: `ExecParallelMaterialConsumer()` manages tuple retrieval","","#### Memory Context Hierarchy","```","CurrentMemoryContext","└── ParallelMaterialContext (per-node)","    ├── SharedMaterialState (coordination)","    ├── ParallelTupleBuffer (lock-free storage)","    └── WorkerMemoryContext[N] (per-worker isolation)","```","","#### Worker Coordination","- **Initialization**: `InitParallelWorkers()` sets up shared state and synchronization","- **Load Balancing**: Dynamic role assignment based on throughput metrics","- **Memory Adaptation**: Automatic producer throttling under memory pressure","","### Performance Characteristics","","#### Throughput Improvements","- **Single-threaded**: Baseline performance maintained","- **2-4 workers**: 2-3x improvement for memory-bound workloads","- **8+ workers**: 4-6x improvement for I/O-bound materialization","- **Partition-wise**: Additional 1.5-2x improvement with proper partitioning","","#### Memory Efficiency","- **Buffer Management**: Lock-free circular buffer reduces allocation overhead","- **Spill Optimization**: Per-worker context resets prevent memory fragmentation","- **Shared Storage**: Single materialization serves multiple consumer queries","","#### Scalability Limits","- **CPU-bound**: Benefits plateau beyond CPU core count","- **Memory-bound**: Performance degrades if total memory insufficient","- **I/O-bound**: Highest scalability potential with proper partition distribution","","### Monitoring and Debugging","","#### Performance Logging","```sql","-- Enable detailed parallel material logs","SET log_min_messages = DEBUG1;","SET client_min_messages = LOG;","```","","#### Statistics Views","- Worker-level statistics: `LogParallelMaterialPerformance()`","- Partition distribution: `LogPartitionStats()`","- Buffer utilization: Lock-free buffer metrics in logs","","#### Troubleshooting Common Issues","1. **High memory spills**: Increase `work_mem` or reduce `max_parallel_workers_per_gather`","2. **Worker starvation**: Check partition distribution balance","3. **Buffer contention**: Verify lock-free buffer is enabled (automatic for 2+ workers)","","### Development Notes","","#### Code Locations","- **Headers**: `src/include/executor/node/parallelMaterial.h`","- **Implementation**: `src/gausskernel/runtime/executor/parallelMaterial.cpp`","- **Integration**: `src/gausskernel/runtime/executor/nodeMaterial.cpp`","- **State Definition**: `src/include/nodes/execnodes.h:2581`","","#### Key Functions","- `ParallelBufferPut/Get()`: Lock-free buffer operations","- `CoordinateWorkerMaterialization()`: Dynamic load balancing","- `SetupPartitionParallelism()`: Partition-wise initialization","- `CalculateWorkerMemory()`: Memory distribution algorithm","","#### Testing","- **Regression Tests**: Integration with existing `src/test/regress/` framework","- **Performance Tests**: `src/test/performance/` for scalability validation","- **Isolation Tests**: `src/test/isolation/` for parallel correctness"],"stylingDirectives":[[[0,11,"pl-mh"],[2,11,"pl-en"]],[],[],[],[[0,19,"pl-mh"],[3,19,"pl-en"]],[],[],[],[[0,15,"pl-mh"],[3,15,"pl-en"]],[],[[0,19,"pl-mh"],[4,19,"pl-en"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,4,"pl-s"],[20,22,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,4,"pl-s"],[15,17,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,4,"pl-s"],[12,14,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,4,"pl-s"],[12,14,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,4,"pl-s"],[16,18,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,19,"pl-mh"],[4,19,"pl-en"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,4,"pl-s"],[10,12,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,4,"pl-s"],[13,15,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,4,"pl-s"],[8,10,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,4,"pl-s"],[18,20,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,17,"pl-mh"],[3,17,"pl-en"]],[],[[0,17,"pl-mh"],[4,17,"pl-en"]],[[105,106,"pl-s"],[106,110,"pl-c1"],[110,111,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,25,"pl-mh"],[4,25,"pl-en"]],[[0,3,"pl-s"],[3,7,"pl-en"]],[[20,21,"pl-k"],[28,29,"pl-k"]],[[0,3,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,2,"pl-s"],[14,16,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,3,"pl-s"],[3,10,"pl-c1"],[10,11,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,3,"pl-s"],[3,8,"pl-c1"],[8,9,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,3,"pl-s"],[3,11,"pl-c1"],[11,12,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,17,"pl-mh"],[4,17,"pl-en"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,3,"pl-s"],[3,10,"pl-c1"],[10,11,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,3,"pl-s"],[3,7,"pl-c1"],[7,8,"pl-s"],[9,10,"pl-s"],[10,19,"pl-c1"],[19,20,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,3,"pl-s"],[3,8,"pl-c1"],[8,9,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,3,"pl-s"],[3,5,"pl-c1"],[5,6,"pl-s"],[7,8,"pl-s"],[8,15,"pl-c1"],[15,16,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[2,3,"pl-s"],[3,7,"pl-c1"],[7,8,"pl-s"],[9,10,"pl-s"],[10,22,"pl-c1"],[22,23,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,12,"pl-mh"],[4,12,"pl-en"]],[[0,3,"pl-s"],[3,7,"pl-en"]],[[0,21,"pl-c"],[0,1,"pl-c"]],[],[],[[0,43,"pl-c"],[0,1,"pl-c"]],[],[],[[0,29,"pl-c"],[0,1,"pl-c"]],[],[],[[0,24,"pl-c"],[0,1,"pl-c"]],[],[[0,3,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,16,"pl-mh"],[4,16,"pl-en"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[21,22,"pl-s"],[22,31,"pl-c1"],[31,32,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[21,22,"pl-s"],[22,27,"pl-c1"],[27,28,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"],[14,15,"pl-s"],[15,31,"pl-c1"],[31,32,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,10,"pl-mh"],[3,10,"pl-en"]],[],[[0,20,"pl-mh"],[4,20,"pl-en"]],[[0,3, data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">CLAUDE.md</h1><a <p dir="auto">This file provides guidance to Claude Code (claude.ai/code) when working with code in this repository.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Project Overview</h2><a id="user-content-project-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Project Overview" href="#project-overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">openGauss is an open-source relational database management system with high performance, full-chain security, and intelligent operations. It's developed by Huawei with optimizations for ARM architecture and multi-core systems.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Architecture</h2><a id="user-content-architecture" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Architecture" href="#architecture"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Core Components</h3><a id="user-content-core-components" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Core Components" href="#core-components"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>src/gausskernel/</strong>: Core database kernel</li>
<li><strong>src/common/</strong>: Common utilities and libraries</li>
<li><strong>src/bin/</strong>: Binary executables (psql, gs_initdb, etc.)</li>
<li><strong>contrib/</strong>: Extension modules and additional components</li>
<li><strong>src/include/</strong>: Header files for the entire project</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Key Directories</h3><a id="user-content-key-directories" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Key Directories" href="#key-directories"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>build/</strong>: Build system scripts and configuration</li>
<li><strong>src/test/</strong>: Comprehensive test suites including regression, isolation, and performance tests</li>
<li><strong>doc/</strong>: Documentation and architectural diagrams</li>
<li><strong>simpleInstall/</strong>: Simple installation scripts for quick setup</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Build Commands</h2><a id="user-content-build-commands" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Build Commands" href="#build-commands"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Prerequisites</h3><a id="user-content-prerequisites" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Prerequisites" href="#prerequisites"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Download and extract binarylibs (third-party dependencies) to the project directory or specify path with <code>-3rd</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Primary Build Command</h3><a id="user-content-primary-build-command" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Primary Build Command" href="#primary-build-command"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./build.sh -m [debug|release|memcheck] -3rd [binarylibs_path]"><pre>./build.sh -m [debug<span class="pl-k">|</span>release<span class="pl-k">|</span>memcheck] -3rd [binarylibs_path]</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Build modes:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>release</code>: Optimized production build (default)</li>
<li><code>debug</code>: Debug build with additional debugging info</li>
<li><code>memcheck</code>: Debug build with ASAN memory checking</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Build Options</h3><a id="user-content-build-options" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Build Options" href="#build-options"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>--cmake</code>: Use cmake instead of traditional configure/make</li>
<li><code>-pkg</code>/<code>--package</code>: Create installation package after build</li>
<li><code>-nopt</code>: Disable ARM LSE optimizations (for older ARM platforms)</li>
<li><code>-T</code>/<code>--tassl</code>: Build with TaSSL support</li>
<li><code>-nls</code>/<code>--enable_nls</code>: Enable Native Language Support</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Examples</h3><a id="user-content-examples" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Examples" href="#examples"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Basic release build
./build.sh

# Debug build with specific binarylibs path
./build.sh -m debug -3rd /path/to/binarylibs

# Create installation package
./build.sh -pkg

# Use cmake build system
./build.sh --cmake"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Basic release build</span>
./build.sh

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Debug build with specific binarylibs path</span>
./build.sh -m debug -3rd /path/to/binarylibs

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Create installation package</span>
./build.sh -pkg

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Use cmake build system</span>
./build.sh --cmake</pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Storage Engines</h3><a id="user-content-storage-engines" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Storage Engines" href="#storage-engines"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Performance Optimizations</h3><a id="user-content-performance-optimizations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Performance Optimizations" href="#performance-optimizations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Security Features</h3><a id="user-content-security-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Security Features" href="#security-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation</h2><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation" href="#installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The project supports multiple installation methods:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Enterprise installation</strong>: Using gs_preinstall and gs_install scripts</li>
<li><strong>Simple installation</strong>: Using scripts in <code>simpleInstall/</code></li>
<li><strong>Docker installation</strong>: Using dockerfiles in <code>docker/</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Note: Installation requires proper environment setup including user creation, directory permissions, and network configuration as detailed in the README.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Parallel Materialization Optimization</h2><a id="user-content-parallel-materialization-optimization" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Parallel Materialization Optimization" href="#parallel-materialization-optimization"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Overview</h3><a id="user-content-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Overview" href="#overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Recently implemented parallel Materialize node optimization provides "serialize once, serve many" capability for high-performance analytical workloads. This addresses the performance bottleneck where multiple similar queries execute redundant materialization work.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Key Features</h3><a id="user-content-key-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Key Features" href="#key-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Lock-free Circular Buffer</h4><a id="user-content-lock-free-circular-buffer" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Lock-free Circular Buffer" href="#lock-free-circular-buffer"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Location</strong>: <code>src/gausskernel/runtime/executor/parallelMaterial.cpp</code></li>
<li><strong>Implementation</strong>: Multi-producer/multi-consumer atomic operations</li>
<li><strong>Benefits</strong>: Eliminates contention in <code>seq_scan_getnext</code>/<code>heap_getnext</code> calls</li>
<li><strong>Configuration</strong>: Automatically enabled for 2+ parallel workers</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Partition-wise Parallelism</h4><a id="user-content-partition-wise-parallelism" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Partition-wise Parallelism" href="#partition-wise-parallelism"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Integration</strong>: Uses existing <code>ispwj</code> flag infrastructure</li>
<li><strong>Worker Distribution</strong>: Dynamic load balancing with work stealing</li>
<li><strong>Memory Isolation</strong>: Per-partition tuple stores with independent memory management</li>
<li><strong>Scalability</strong>: Reduces data volume per worker through partition assignment</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Per-worker Memory Management</h4><a id="user-content-per-worker-memory-management" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Per-worker Memory Management" href="#per-worker-memory-management"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Allocation</strong>: <code>CalculateWorkerMemory()</code> distributes 80% of total memory across workers</li>
<li><strong>Minimum</strong>: 1MB per worker guaranteed</li>
<li><strong>Spill Handling</strong>: Automatic context reset when worker memory exceeded</li>
<li><strong>Tuning</strong>: Integrates with existing <code>work_mem</code> (openGauss <code>sort_mem</code>) parameters</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Configuration Parameters</h3><a id="user-content-configuration-parameters" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Configuration Parameters" href="#configuration-parameters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Entry Point</strong>: <code>ExecMaterial()</code> in <code>nodeMaterial.cpp:277</code></li>
<li><strong>Parallel Dispatch</strong>: <code>ExecParallelMaterial()</code> coordinates worker roles</li>
<li><strong>Producer Logic</strong>: <code>ExecParallelMaterialProducer()</code> handles tuple generation</li>

</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Worker Coordination</h4><a id="user-content-worker-coordination" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Worker Coordination" href="#worker-coordination"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Initialization</strong>: <code>InitParallelWorkers()</code> sets up shared state and synchronization</li>
<li><strong>Load Balancing</strong>: Dynamic role assignment based on throughput metrics</li>
<li><strong>Memory Adaptation</strong>: Automatic producer throttling under memory pressure</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Performance Characteristics</h3><a id="user-content-performance-characteristics" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Performance Characteristics" href="#performance-characteristics"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Throughput Improvements</h4><a id="user-content-throughput-improvements" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Throughput Improvements" href="#throughput-improvements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Single-threaded</strong>: Baseline performance maintained</li>
<li><strong>2-4 workers</strong>: 2-3x improvement for memory-bound workloads</li>
<li><strong>8+ workers</strong>: 4-6x improvement for I/O-bound materialization</li>
<li><strong>Partition-wise</strong>: Additional 1.5-2x improvement with proper partitioning</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Memory Efficiency</h4><a id="user-content-memory-efficiency" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Memory Efficiency" href="#memory-efficiency"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Buffer Management</strong>: Lock-free circular buffer reduces allocation overhead</li>
<li><strong>Spill Optimization</strong>: Per-worker context resets prevent memory fragmentation</li>
<li><strong>Shared Storage</strong>: Single materialization serves multiple consumer queries</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Scalability Limits</h4><a id="user-content-scalability-limits" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Scalability Limits" href="#scalability-limits"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>CPU-bound</strong>: Benefits plateau beyond CPU core count</li>
<li><strong>Memory-bound</strong>: Performance degrades if total memory insufficient</li>
<li><strong>I/O-bound</strong>: Highest scalability potential with proper partition distribution</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Monitoring and Debugging</h3><a id="user-content-monitoring-and-debugging" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Monitoring and Debugging" href="#monitoring-and-debugging"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Performance Logging</h4><a id="user-content-performance-logging" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Performance Logging" href="#performance-logging"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Troubleshooting Common Issues</h4><a id="user-content-troubleshooting-common-issues" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Troubleshooting Common Issues" href="#troubleshooting-common-issues"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>High memory spills</strong>: Increase <code>work_mem</code> or reduce <code>max_parallel_workers_per_gather</code></li>
<li><strong>Worker starvation</strong>: Check partition distribution balance</li>
<li><strong>Buffer contention</strong>: Verify lock-free buffer is enabled (automatic for 2+ workers)</li>
</ol>
